Spring and Autumn

Journey on the Yangtze River

— Gan Xiao

The twentieth century should be the era of "man conquering nature," but in many, many places in our daily lives, we are always "calling out to heaven in desperation."

This time, I came from Hankou, from river to river, which was originally a very smooth waterway, but I called out to heaven several times; and even after arriving home safely, I still felt like an old woman from the countryside, feeling "blessed by heaven."

Buying a boat ticket with money is the simplest thing, but I still called out to heaven. On the day I arrived in Hankou, several boats were docked along the riverbank, and goods and passengers had already been unloaded completely. However, the larger ones belonged to the state-owned China Merchants Bureau and had already been assigned as "official boats." The smaller boats belonged to private companies, and the official ticket sales time only lasted for a few fleeting minutes, so one had to go to the black market. And a friend working at the shipping company listed a large number of unstable aspects of black market tickets, which made me, a law-abiding citizen, have to cautiously retreat. "An honest person doesn't do shady things," I followed my friend's advice and waited for a "official market" ticket to arrive. As a result, I waited and waited, and the rats and bedbugs in the warehouse attacked wantonly. I was so anxious that my hair turned white, and I firmly advocated sacrificing to the "black market" to eat. Only then did I buy a third-class "fixed cabin" ticket (with a bunk) at one and a half times the price. First and second-class tickets had naturally been given to the "black market".

The boat I was on couldn't be considered young: it was fifty-three years old! Stepping onto the deck, the soles of my feet were sticky, indicating that it was well-worn and weathered, not a tender, white-skinned beginner. It was said to weigh about five hundred tons, and it loaded three or four hundred tons of goods and four or five hundred passengers in Hankou; most of the passengers were demobilized military and government personnel, surrounded by boxes and miscellaneous items, so the boat was quite full. There were not many first and second-class passengers, most of them were third-class "fixed cabin" and fourth-class "open cabin." How could people not call out to heaven when all these people had to be crammed into this fish gut!

The "fixed cabin" bunks were divided into upper and lower layers, and mine was on the lower layer. I turned sideways to open the quilt and spread it out, and put a few small luggage items at my feet. In order to reduce crowding, I took off my leather shoes and burrowed into the quilt. Then a series of noises came, mostly about the excessive luggage of the passengers, and the steward tried his best to stop them. What was the use of the stewards? They didn't have grass-green uniforms and collar badges; as a result, the "fixed cabin" became a disguised luggage room, and all the air vents and passageways were blocked by luggage. And the most wonderful thing was my "head people": there were a total of eleven of them, and they only bought four upper bunks; two bunks were prepared for people to sit on; and two bunks were prepared to place those twenty-five or six pieces of luggage! When they put down six bayonet-mounted rifles, the stewards all shut their mouths and stood far away, and the luggage was moved in piece by piece. I was lying on my back looking up and could see very clearly: the luggage bunk was gradually tilting, and the only crossbar was gradually bending. I knew that the two female passengers sleeping in the lower bunks were in extreme danger, and I couldn't help but stand up and protest. I said:

"This is not a luggage room. If everyone puts luggage in like this, the air will be completely squeezed out. And putting these luggage items on these thin boards will cause the upper bunk to collapse and kill people. Who will take responsibility?"

Hey! Their leader stood out conspicuously, patted his chest: "I'll take responsibility, I'm a brigade commander!" He pointed to his major general collar badge. Oh! Brigade commander! I thought to myself: "The brigade commander fell from the sky, what does he care about killing people or not killing people?" In the midst of thinking this, the crossbar really broke. If there weren't also boxes and baskets on the lower female passengers' bunks, those two women would have had to test the brigade commander's "responsibility." I don't know how, I heavily tapped that brigadier's shoulder, without saying a word, just pressed the flashlight to show him the broken crossbar. His arrogance was a little lower at this time, and he directed his soldiers: "Move the luggage down! There's going to be a death case!" So all his luggage was stuffed in the passageway, and the four bunks only slept eleven people, so we "lower people" were spared from the disaster of being crushed to death, and we had to thank heaven and earth!

The next morning, it was time to go to the women's restroom: walk along the stern to the kitchen, walk down the steps from the kitchen, pass through the open-cabin bunks, and turn right. Open that short door, and the situation inside was unbearable to look at: it was obvious that excrement and urine were flowing straight down; there was no room to stand. Good heavens, the "black slave ships" of the sixteenth and seventeenth centuries must have been like this!

Climbing up the handrail, a pile of people squatted down and blocked the way. Looking down, they were all holding rice with both hands on the floor. One pile of rice was knocked over, and the white rice was mixed with the black paste that stained the bottom of the feet, like the sesame filling of pig lard glutinous rice balls; good heavens! This is what they were preparing for the third and fourth-class passengers to eat!

I wanted to go to the deck for a breath of fresh air, but this boat had no deck at all. Looking at it, it was all piles of firewood like mountains! The "open cabin" friends were all learning Goujian's lying on firewood, using the firewood as bunks. Besides the firewood, there were dozens and hundreds of baskets of eggs, duck eggs, salted fish, and cured meat. I asked an old steward and learned that these were the private goods of the boat's accountants and stewards. I asked him why he could bring so many private goods? He frowned and smiled bitterly and said: "What else can we do if we don't bring them? There are a total of thirty-five stewards, and none of us have a big money salary. The boat only provides a mouthful of white rice, and everyone at home has children and wives. Now most of the passengers are soldiers, and we can't get tea money by soliciting tips. What else can we do if we don't bring private goods? Now it's concealing from the top but not from the bottom. Besides the company's big boss, the boat's accountants are all in the same boat. The accountants have salaries, and they can also sell bunks on the boat; but the private goods they bring are even more than ours." I couldn't estimate how much their private goods weighed, but when I poked my head out and looked down, the calm river water was almost level with the ship's side, and a small wave could hit the porthole. This old small boat was really in danger.

The teacher taught people "not to stand under a dangerous wall." We are now loaded on a dangerous boat, surrounded by the vast river, what other way to be at ease other than secretly calling out to heaven?

After passing Datong, it suddenly anchored in the middle of the night, and everyone asked the steward one after another. The old steward explained; "There's fog! Fog is falling from the sky. The boat's salary is low; the pilot is an inexperienced greenhorn. This is called blind eyes not minding clubfoot, and clubfoot not minding blind eyes, so they just accommodate each other. At this time, it's good to be careful and stop." Good heavens, anchoring is good! Otherwise, we would have sacrificed to their "blindness" and "clubfoot"!

Approaching Jiangyin, it anchored again. The impatient passengers all jumped up. The old steward came to explain again: "Passengers, you are anxious, our pilot is more anxious than you, he has a celebration at home tomorrow night. There's no way! The boat is about to reach 'Anchor Sand,' it's getting dark, and the fog is heavy, how can we go? Other foreign ships have to be careful too. And say our 'old grandfather ship'! A few passengers asked him: "What is 'Anchor Sand'?" "Anchor Sand"? "Anchor Sand" is weird! It's a monster! In the middle of the night, it comes together, and the boat runs aground. When it dawns, the sand sinks down, and the boat is sucked down together. There used to be a French boat that ran aground in Dao Place, thinking it was okay, but it was sucked away by the monster at dawn. Only when the Japanese are here, the monsters are also afraid of them and never appear." Are monsters really afraid of the Japanese? I think there are more lighthouses!

It anchored for two hours, and the engine started wheezing again. The fog became heavier and heavier, and the riverbank was nowhere to be seen. The whistle sounded a long blast every two minutes, and the long blasts sounded like the dying wails of wild beasts, so disturbing! The old steward was complaining like a monologue: "Looking for death! Sailing in such fog! If we make it through, the pilot alone will be happy to be a new groom, if we don't make it through, five hundred people will be happy to see King Yama together!" Late at night, a dim oil lamp swayed, and the prone passengers looked like corpses, the steward's complaints and the wailing whistle intertwined, making people shudder, as if King Yama was waving.

Finally, it dawned, and the sun was about to break through the clouds and fog. Although the riverbank was still invisible, the whistle sounded less and less. After a few more hours, it finally brought us to the Huangpu River bank. When we stepped ashore, we were even more fortunate to be reborn, as if we had entered heaven.

The river is so dark and without sunlight, going on the river in the twentieth century, everyone still relies on heaven, who would want to be born in this time and place?

"Fruit" Original Manuscript

— Botticelli

Botticelli (Sandro Botticelli 1445-1510) can be considered an outstanding talent full of imagination in the Florentine school. Although he also painted several Madonna and Child pictures, he was a bold anti-Christian. His representative works include "Allegory of Spring" and "The Birth of Venus". The composition is especially clever and ingenious, the colors are fresh and the lines are beautiful. Although the subject matter belongs to fantasy, the faces are full of desire and have a "modern" feeling. The original manuscript of "Fruit" is one of them. (Lion)

Winter Solstice Grass

— Liu Sui

It is the time when dreams return.

The cold wind outside the window howls.

The clamorous noises have quieted down, and the memories by the pillow turn again toward a sorrowful life. A clear blockage has formed in my heart.

I seem to hear your soft laughter:

"Your journey through life is gradually becoming dim and shrinking!"

Yes, it's been a year already, precisely today, the day when people at the Qiantang Riverhead were immersed in rare revelry. The warmth of peace and light unveiled our curtains, and we slowly walked across that long and peaceful lakeside embankment, as if traversing a period of suffering that had already distanced itself from us. There was the radiance of lights deep within the willow grove, and I saw the excitement and joy rising and falling in your chest:

"From now on, you should stumble forward vividly and stubbornly towards the journey you desire!"

"Quietly," my lips imprinted on your warm hairline, "I am thinking about those splendid and extravagant steps ahead!"

A corner of the small building conveyed melodious singing, the lake water was still silent, and the night mist drifted across our cheeks; we smiled at each other.

Can you say that was a distant dream?

In the third month of spring this year, I came to this city with you.

I heard people praising the blessings of this newborn city.

But I saw many things:

The people who came from the distant northern lands, apart from still harboring some warm memories of the hearth in the snowy sky, have they not all learned to extract tender vows along the edges of those busy, bustling canopies?

And also those who came to this city, huddled from the south, the longing and attachment to the azure seas and cloudless skies have already faded away, and in many corners that attract people to linger, are they not also composing melodies that make people feel lost, using the sound of joyful hearts?

Who understands lament? Who understands anger? Are we not all hastily and confusedly crafting things that mock our lives with our own hands?

Helplessly, I ran through every corner of this city again and again, and the accusations of the virtuous were suffocated to the point of near extinction! Harm to society exists everywhere! Oppression of humanity!

There is no story, no poems, just a page of lamentable blankness!

It was originally a bottomless turbid flow!

Gradually, I forgot how to sing loudly and shout wildly, and I slowly learned the worldly ways and pretenses of life; I accepted the society's praise and indulgence, and I also tasted the melancholy and sorrow of the human world. I have become a piece of flotsam floating in the turbid flow; flotsam will never, and cannot, cause ripples in the turbid flow!

The vivid and stubborn journey is no longer intimate, and a shameful emptiness remains in my heart.

This disappointment to you is inevitable.

However, I am already tired enough.

Yes, it has been a year, precisely today. The people in this city have not diminished their usual revelry, desolate songs are still overflowing, and emerald green cypress branches and ivy reflect the flames in the candle tears, all of which deeply evoke my nostalgia.

Let repentance wash away my year of idleness and procrastination! Even if this city inflicts cruelty and bitterness upon me, there is still next year, and there is still a precious period of time... I still have a soul that has not been infected by vulgarity and decadence!

I silently pondered beside the pillow, facing the candle. You should be able to imagine my feelings at this moment.

The clamorous human world will be restored again, right? The cold wind outside the window howls.

You should bless it, the future rebirth of this city!

It is the time when dreams return.

The eve of the Winter Solstice, Year 35.

An Inch of River, an Inch of Blood 134

— Ye Jingfeng

"Oh!" For the first time, Tsurumi felt real terror. "Then where did these numbers come from?"

"That was probably a year ago?"

"What?" Tsurumi thought he had misheard.

"You know we also have a set of machines. A year ago, we often received this kind of special code but didn't pay much attention. In the past year, we've heard more about it. Teacher Aoki spent some effort to crack the numbers... But you don't need to worry. So far, only he alone can decipher them, but it still takes a lot of effort. He doesn't want to publish it, and he doesn't want to do it much. He doesn't want to waste his energy. He says he still wants to live."

"Ah," Tsurumi heard this and felt a weight lifted from his shoulders. "Pingzi, I have one more thing to say. What I'm doing is so difficult. Since the old gentleman says someone else is also doing it, this is a virtuous act that saves countless lives. Why doesn't the old gentleman..."

"Why not find that thing?" Pingzi finished Tsurumi's sentence. "It's not that he doesn't want to find it, but he can't find the location where it's hidden."

"Why not use metaphysics?"

"Brother, you say you've also studied metaphysics. How can you say such unprofessional things?"

"Couldn't he perform the art on the person hiding it?"

"There's no medium."

"Aren't you a ready-made medium?"

"I have no feelings for that old fellow. How can I be a medium?" Pingzi was a little angry.

"Ah!" Tsurumi was disappointed. "Then, goodbye."

"Goodbye, brother. Definitely goodbye. At least three times; the last goodbye, I hear, will be very long!" Pingzi hung up the phone with a chuckle.

Tsurumi was preoccupied and didn't pay much attention to the meaning of Pingzi's "long time," nor did he want to argue with her any further. Although the evening's plan had been disturbed by this phone call, everyone felt that things had reached this stage, and it was like an arrow on the string, which had to be launched. Besides, they were somewhat skeptical of Pingzi's words.

At exactly nine o'clock in the evening, Tsurumi was already sitting upright in the military aircraft "Chang Sheng". There were seven or eight people traveling with him, all senior active-duty officers going to North China, except for Tsurumi. However, half an hour before the plane took off, the second supplemental edition of Tokyo's evening newspapers all carried a mysterious short message, titled "Challenge to Tsurumi Wang by a Mysterious Adversary," which read: "Tsurumi Tama-kun: I have long admired your good skills as a man. Now you are in a time of turmoil. The Prime Minister also favors you with a discerning eye; a meteoric rise is within reach. However, although my colleagues are of humble origins, we do not presume to be superior. We have something to suggest, presumptuously seeking a small price; swordsmanship, archery, grant us one or two skills, and it will be enough. Around eleven o'clock in the evening, 'Beppu' will be waiting sincerely. Bowing, the members of the Sino Society."

On that day, the evening newspapers all treated this matter as fresh material. After publishing this mysterious short message, the editors of each newspaper added a few thoughts: some said, "Why are they fighting each other?" Others said, "The style of the knights of the Edo fifteenth century is seen again today!" Still others said, "A chivalrous thief is challenging Sherlock Holmes; there is sure to be a good show to watch!" And some said, "Soldiers should serve the country loyally, and should do their best, not seek merit. Why be jealous? If you feel indignant, you should be upright and stand up and compare your strengths in front of the public, not rely on sneaky tricks," and so on.

On the plane, five or six out of the eight passengers had bought several copies of the second supplemental edition; although the newspapers were different, they all carried this short message, and it was explained that Tsurumi was on this "Wei Sheng" aircraft. Although the seven people did not know Tsurumi, they could certainly guess; because they were a group, and Tsurumi was alone.

Homecoming Poetry

— Pin Baihua

Awakening Wang Wei cannot paint it,

I should be able to boast that my birthplace has a "famous mountain". China is a country with many mountains, but a mountain must be clear and beautiful to be considered famous. So, Li Taibai, the immortal banished to earth over a thousand years ago, did not distort the line of poetry, "Loving famous mountains, I enter into the lands of Yue"; at the same time, he also dreamed of traveling to Mount Tianmu, the so-called "eighteen thousand feet" place of the banished immortal's dream journey is located to the east of my hometown. But things often turn out to be the opposite. Regarding the famous mountain of my birthplace, for more than ten years, feelings of cherishing have overshadowed elements of self-praise, because I have long become a "person of the east, west, north, and south", without the fortune of "riding a gentle steed, traveling in a low carriage, and being a virtuous person in my hometown".

However, I have finally returned. After passing "Qingfeng Ridge", the Yan Stream is like a smooth ribbon, circling around the towering peaks and white clouds, which are the outer garments of the mountain spirits! It floats so freely over one mountain peak after another. The lush trees screen a few white-walled houses, telling me that this is a natural embrace without the machinations of the city. I think that this not only attracts the poetic inspiration of the banished immortal, but it is also a very good painting, but so good that it is too natural. Unless Wang Mojie, whose "paintings have poetry", comes to create a "Yue Zhong Diagram", wouldn't it be better than the "Axis River Diagram" where "mountain valleys are dense and clouds fly and move"?

The small chartered car stopped in Sheng County. I knew that Zongen took advantage of the remaining time before changing cars to take a look at "Listening Pavilion," but it was just a mound of earth covered with weeds. In such a place, how many people can learn from Dai Andao by "having both oranges and a dou of wine"? Naturally, it was deep autumn, where could one find yellow orioles? We circled around the edge of the grassy area, and then we got on the bus to Xinchang. Shengxin is only forty miles apart, and the carriage was filled with the sounds of the local dialect, but after more than ten years of separation, even my local dialect has changed, not to mention the hair on my temples. Especially in a cloth gown, who would recognize you? So I huddled up, afraid to listen to the local dialect. Gradually, the ancient mountain city of my hometown came into view. I pulled Zongen and jumped out of the car, and we walked along the secluded road at the foot of the city, not wanting the "elders of Jiangdong" to discover this poor boy returning to his hometown as old as ever.

It was night, and my hometown had no electric lights. I remember that in the past, there was this gift from the city, but perhaps "restoration" is not easy! Thus, when night falls, the whole place is pitch black. In addition, seven or eight tenths of the streets and houses were destroyed in the calamity, leaving a field of rubble. Although we carried a "lantern" to walk, it was still very difficult to find the path. My three old houses had become "truly" dilapidated, with nothing inside. I temporarily lodged in the empty house of the Assembly.

For several days in a row, I was fortunate to have Zongen's help, so that eating was not a problem, because there were people inviting us to dinner every morning and evening. However, I was disgusted that the invitation cards actually had the words "Professor Lu" written after "Inspector Chen". In this small mountain city, where civil servants earn at most three or four hundred thousand yuan a month, and the county magistrate earns no more than one million, the pomp and entertainment were surprisingly urbanized.

A thousand stacks of emerald green bathe my lapel,

Awakening Wang Wei cannot paint it;

Returning in scholar's robes, no one recognizes me,

The carriage behind fears the prolonged sound of my hometown!

After ten years of barrenness, I seek the three paths,

Wood and stone are heartless and easily change masters;

I wish to sacrifice to the Dragon Mound as an unfilial son,

Stone pass trees planted of all kinds transform and grow.

A Brief History of Musicians

Handel

— Tian

Handel, a great German musician, is as famous as Bach, another great musician from the same country. The difference between the two is: Bach lived a secluded life, devoting all his efforts to church music works, whose mood contained strictness in tranquility; Handel was famous throughout Europe, writing opera works with a soaring and fluent pen. However, Handel's place of effort was not Germany, but England. His more important works are considered to be in the "Oratorio". What is called "Oratorio" is similar in nature to opera, but it is not performed on stage, but sung and played by itself. Handel was born in 1683 and died in 1759.

Bach

Bach, a German, is considered the progenitor of modern Western music, and is as famous as Handel. Most of his works are church music, but they are often played in music as well. He wrote extensively throughout his life. Born in 1685, died in 1750.

Page 12

Free Talk

Mishap

— Shaofu

On Christmas Day, three planes crashed in Shanghai one after another, killing and injuring more than seventy people. This tragedy occurred on this festive occasion, which is truly unfortunate!

The cause of the accident was due to the heavy fog, which made it impossible for the planes to identify the airport, resulting in the disaster. After inspecting the wreckage of the planes, there was no sign of fire or burning, which is sufficient to prove that each plane had circled over Shanghai for a long time, and the fuel had been exhausted, forcing them to make an emergency landing. On this day, only China Company's No. 147 aircraft was unexpectedly lucky, and was able to make a forced landing at Jiangwan Airport, suffering slight damage, and the personnel on board were fortunately unharmed.

Fatalists may exaggerate and say: life and death are predetermined. In fact, although this misfortune is said to be the unpredictable wind and clouds of heaven (heavy fog), attributable to changes in the climate, it can still be avoided by doing everything possible. We remember that when the China Clipper was test flying the Pacific route, it encountered a storm on the Pacific Ocean. If it were not for the perfect flight equipment, it would not have been able to complete this flight smoothly. Heavy fog is certainly a major obstacle to flight. If wireless radio is used to guide the direction, and if the ground guidance landing equipment (using light or sound) is perfect, how can heavy fog affect safety?

This year, the record of flight accidents is really not small. If this continues, it is inevitable that the general public will become wary of air travel. Should airline companies and transportation authorities carefully study this matter, and assess all equipment and various responsible personnel (including pilots, communications, and ground personnel) to prevent problems before they occur? Because human life is at stake, there must be no negligence. Seeking perfection is not only providing guarantees to passengers, but also making the greatest contribution to the future of China's aviation industry.

Year-End Mutterings

— Cishou

"Rising winds", "Hitting winds", "Seizing winds", "Overturning winds", "When the great wind rises, the people suffer!"

The 35th year of the Republic of China is about to pass. As we welcome the arrival of the 36th year, we might as well review this year. I think about it again and again, and I can't come up with a good term to give to this year. I might as well give it a "nickname" and call this year the "Year of Many Winds".

Although the weather has been cold recently, the winds outside have not been that strong. Why call it the "Year of Many Winds"? Am I stirring up trouble? Indeed, the meaning of "wind" is very broad; the winds I am talking about are neither the southeast wind nor the northwest wind, but rather the "rising winds", "hitting winds", "seizing winds", and "overturning winds" of this year.

First, the "rising winds". Whenever a rising wind sweeps over, people are as if in a daze, at a loss. When the rising wind has passed, they wake up and take a breath. But good times don't last long. The second rising wind intensifies and comes one after another, putting people back into a state of confusion. The small people live their lives in these endlessly cycling rising winds, and they really don't know when prices will stop rising.

Next, the "hitting winds". Whether you are in a theater or on a sports field, you can see this kind of wind, constantly being directed by someone. I don't know why human nature has become so irritable. People start fighting at the slightest disagreement, beating each other to a bloody pulp, all "as if nothing happened," happy to be watched by others.

Third is the "seizing winds". This year, it is difficult to solve the problem of livelihood, and there are not a few people who take risks, and the seizing winds are becoming more and more intense. But there are different kinds of seizing methods. "Robbers and bandits" rob openly, while corrupt officials and treacherous merchants rob secretly. Those who rob openly say that they are robbing because it is difficult to solve the problem of livelihood, but what are those who rob secretly doing it for? Robbing gold, robbing US dollars, robbing materials, robbing with pleasure. No matter what the robbing method is, privately lining one's pockets will not be as "inflated" as the currency. The more you rob, the more you spend, causing each other, and the robbing is endless!

Finally, let's talk about the "overturning winds". This seems to be the "grand finale". As the end of the year approaches, overturning winds are prevalent.

Liu Jianxu, Chairman of Fujian

— Ganlai

The current Chairman of Fujian Province, Liu Jianxu, graduated from the Third Term of the Baoding Military Academy as an infantry officer. After leaving the school, he served in various military posts, rising from platoon leader to group army commander and deputy commander of the Third War Zone. After the 17th year of the Republic of China, he was responsible for the pacification work on the border between Hunan and Jiangxi, repeatedly achieving the effect of destroying and clearing, which was highly praised by his superiors. During the Anti-Japanese War, he galloped on the southeastern battlefield. In the Battle of Hangzhou Bay, he captured Zhenhai, and the situation in Zhejiang Province was immediately turned from danger to safety. After that, he let Chen Yi become the chairman of Fujian Province, and the lost coastal areas were immediately recovered one by one. He has always adhered to the principle of "three points military, seven points politics" in his administration. The gradual stability of the situation in Fujian shows that his administration has indeed partially achieved results.

In mid-March of this year, Liu passed through Shanghai and hosted a banquet at the Jinmen Hotel for his fellow villagers from Fujian who lived in Shanghai. He himself is from Liling, Hunan, with a fat, round face, which particularly showed his full spirit.

Liu's first wife, Chen, had thirteen daughters and five sons, making up a neat number of ten children in the family.

He governs his family very strictly, does not allow his family members to wear strange clothes, and strongly hates gambling, and uses this as a transformation strategy to see his daughters.

Since the 25th year of the Republic of China, the people of Fujian have suffered from natural disasters, man-made disasters, and corruption and exploitation. Now they need to rest and recover, and the people all deeply hope that Chairman Liu will work hard to govern, stabilize the people's livelihood!

Amidst the Flames of War, There is a Paradise

—

The housing shortage that came with the victory still cannot be resolved even now, a serious problem. The authorities seem to have put some thought into it, and plans have been drawn up one after another, residential areas, people's villages, these are forever just talking on paper.

Recently, I was like "Columbus" discovering a new continent, and I saw a genuine "people's village". Where is it? The location is near "West Station" and "New Longhua". The residents here seem to be like those in "Peach Blossom Spring", living without contention with the world, working at sunrise and resting at sunset.

This place was originally wasteland, but now, shop owners complain of hardship, and factory owners sigh of poverty, saying that the end of the year is difficult to pass, and there is another hurdle after one hurdle. These days, they have a feeling of "every day is like a year", and every day is like "New Year's Eve". I think that if we don't fundamentally think about settling down and unifying, no matter what wise methods you come up with, it will not be able to withstand this overturning wind.

I don't know what kind of wind will come after the overturning wind. In short, this year is the "Year of Many Winds". To be honest, we small people do not miss this kind of year; our only hope is that next year will be "good weather and abundant harvest, the country will be peaceful and the people will be safe", and that we small people will no longer suffer!

It has long become a new "people's village". The newly built houses are not three-dimensional red tile bricks, but they are very neat and orderly, and each household is independent, living very freely and comfortably, with bedrooms, kitchens, living rooms, and some beans, wheat, vegetables, and green onions planted on the open space outside the door. Although there is no tap water, it is not a problem to dig a pond for drinking, and each household raises some chickens, ducks, pigs, and sheep. Therefore, the New Year's dishes may be richer than those of the salaried Shanghainese.

According to friends, the houses here do not need to be "topped" with gold bars. They are all built by fellow villagers from northern Jiangsu themselves, and the building materials needed are moved from rubble yards elsewhere. The old traders said that they lived so comfortably without spending a penny, and they didn't need the dangerous mouths of the second landlords, and they didn't need to pay rent. "Donations and taxes" were like a horse and a cow to them. Although the landlords had negotiated with them, these fellow villagers from northern Jiangsu really had nowhere to live. As the saying goes, there is only a house to keep people living in, not to demolish the house and drive people out, and everyone has a heart of compassion!

In this new "people's village", there are also several village shops, cigarette paper shops, small teahouses, barber shops, and pancake stalls, which are small but complete.

From here, I saw the self-reliance of the people of northern Jiangsu. Each fellow villager from northern Jiangsu can endure hardship and is hardworking, has no dependency, and can "not ask for help" in every place to live. The children already know how to "scavenge" and sell tea without relying on their parents for food and drink, so I think the people of northern Jiangsu are very worthy of emulation.

Tail Feeding Dog

— Gialing

A tax collector delivered a grand speech to many people: "The government and the people are like father and son. Protecting children from being bullied by enemies, educating them, and maintaining them all require money, so the people enthusiastically pay taxes, the more the better, it is really a matter of course!"

One of them listened and said: "I understand, it's like this."

"I keep a puppy. It is hungry and wags its tail at me begging for food. I said to it: 'Dear puppy, you must be very hungry, right? I'm sorry, let me feed you.'"

"I found a knife, cut off its little tail, and sent it to its mouth: 'Eat! My loyal good dog! Eat this piece of meat and replenish your body,' "

The tax collector stopped talking.

Heroic combat posture of French boxing champion Marcel Cerdan.

Democracy and Republic

— Hu Yisheng

In China, there is only "democracy" and no republic. This democracy lacking a republic is just "I am the only one", "I am here". "I" is the most pleasing "note" in the world.

Originally, the trend of the world has universally shifted from individualism to collectivism, but our country is still seeking a way out in the "democracy" of individualism. What can we find out? Adding a lot of "democratic gimmicks" and new bureaucrats who eat "democratic" meals, what is the benefit to China? Wu Zhi Lao said that if you want to achieve world harmony, you must go through thirty-six small wars and seventy-two major wars. With this kind of "democracy" going on, even after seventy-two small wars and one hundred and forty-four major wars, "small harmony" will not come!

I think that China's way out is not in democracy but in a republic, at least it must be said: "A republic is more important than democracy".

Treating Guests

— Zimin

"Hurry! Hurry! Hurry!..." A speeding car drove from afar.

A food carrier slowly walked towards the center of the road.

"Stop! Stop! Stop!"

The food carrier was indifferent and continued to walk towards the center of the road.

"Ghost!" With a sharp sound, the car suddenly braked to a halt.

A head poked out of the small window.

"Hey! Friend, are you preparing to treat guests?"

Shanghai Cross-Section

The Organization of Beggars 20

— Huang Jiamo

Performing Arts and Begging (Continued)

(6) "The True and False Dumbs" — Dumbness is a type of disability, and the beggar gangs also use it as a magic weapon for begging for sympathy. However, there are true and false ones, and the profession is divided into four types. They are called "Hiding from Heaven," "Crying Mouth," "Blocking the Road," and "Acting Real." "Hiding from Heaven" are genuinely mute beggars, while "Crying Mouth" are those who have learned the trick. Pretending to be mute is originally the easiest trick, and their begging is divided into two factions: "Blocking the Road" and "Street Walking." They go their separate ways and do not interfere with each other. "Blocking the Road" involves kneeling by the roadside, knocking their heads on the ground, chanting something, pointing to heaven and earth, then pointing to their own mouths and hearts, patting their chests to beg. "Street Walking" involves begging from house to house. False dumbs gather when begging, and are not allowed to talk as a rule, only being allowed to speak after returning to the "Imperial Incense Hall" (beggar factory).

(7) "Nose Guanyin" — This group must wear straw shoes and tie straw rings on their heads. "Double Dragons Entering the Sea" involves using bamboo to carve two long objects, suspending tassels on the ends. When begging, they insert the bamboo into their nostrils, exposing the tassels outside. "True Dragon Entering the Mouth" is about putting a snake through the nose. Both factions "breathe through one nostril."

(8) "Sitting and Cursing" — With crippled limbs, they sit by the roadside cursing wildly. Their curse goes: "Good feet, good hands, the road to heaven; bad feet, bad hands, the gate to hell. Out in the open, secretly coming, not a penny wasted on empty ground." The singing is full of ups and downs, making people feel pity.

(9) "Selling Ear Picks" — Selling bamboo ear picks along the street is another branch of the beggar gang. The gang calls themselves "Holding a Gauze Hat," not knowing where the meaning comes from. But those who work this profession are unwilling to admit that they are beggars. Probably because the income is not bad, they have already joined the ranks of small vendors. It is said that one must be able to hold a gauze hat with the right hand and be able to independently use a knife to manufacture with the left hand to be considered a family skill.

(10) "Bitter Flesh Knife" — This gang is divided into two types: "Waist Blocking" and "Enclosure." When a "Waist Blocking" beggar goes to the street, they must first wear the upper body and carry a two-foot-long disciplinary knife. When not given money, they would strike their waist hard, leaving new red marks. Making the shopkeepers both surprised and pitying, giving money to end the matter. "Enclosure" is similar to street performances, setting up a venue on the roadside wasteland, asking people for donations. However, these people do not have the good skills of the Jianghu gangs, just randomly bang and knock for a while, deceiving idle people.

(11) "Dancing Single Stick" — Similar to the above, they belong to the sub-category of Jianghu street performances, but are despised by the Jianghu gangs. One type is called "Neat Attributes," which can dance the wooden stick in a variety of ways. Another type is called "Beating Single Stick," which uses three short sticks, one thick and two thin, dancing and begging along the street.

(12) "The True and False Blinds" — If there are true and false dumbs, there must be true and false blinds, and the false blinds are more than the true blinds. The fake goods are called "Cold Look" in the gang, which is also a wonderful metaphor. Holding a bamboo pole, the eyelids turned outwards, hiding the black pupils, it is admirable that they still understand makeup skills. The street call has a saying: "Raise your head and not see the road to heaven, lift your feet and not see the height of the road." Such things cannot be fully remembered. "Rotten Beauty" sitting and begging also belongs to this gang. On the surface, it is covered with sores, displayed on the roadside for exhibition. In fact, most of them use the makeup skills passed down from the beggar gang. In addition, there are those who kneel by the roadside knocking their heads, knocking their foreheads into giant blocks like walnuts. Also belongs to this gang, to be described in detail later.

As the End of the Year Approaches, Wang Xiaoer Runs Away

— Wu Shujiang

"I, Wang Xiaoer, am unfortunate to have the surname Wang, and also unfortunate to be named Xiaoer, so in the past, people in society, such as when national affairs were not done well, or the business market was sluggish, they themselves did not work hard, and they all used me, Wang Xiaoer, to make fun of, 'Wang Xiaoer celebrating the New Year,' 'worse every year.'

I, Wang Xiaoer, am just a bit poor, I have not done anything that endangers the country, nor have I done the manipulation and speculation tricks done by unscrupulous merchants. Why is it that when national affairs are not done well, I am used to make fun of them, and when the business market is sluggish, I am also used to make fun of them. Since I, Xiaoer, entered the Republic of China, it is difficult to encounter the end of the year without hearing these insulting words to me, I am really angry.

Now the War of Resistance has been won, and it has been more than a year since the victory. National affairs should gradually be on the right track, and the future of the country is close to a bright and glorious situation. What about the business market? With the guidance and supervision of the government, it will of course be calm and prosperous day by day. What about the people? After this long victory in the War of Resistance, they must of course work hard, become strong, and become new citizens. When I, Wang Xiaoer, welcome the thirty-sixth year with national rejoicing, I formally bid farewell to the people of the country, forever farewell, and I sincerely hope that there will be no Wang Xiaoer in this society from now on, and I also hope that from now on, when things go wrong in society, do not use me, Wang Xiaoer, to make fun of them."
